---
about_this_resource_text: "<p><strong>Description:</strong> After proving Roth&rsquo;s\
  \ theorem last lecture, Professor Zhao explains Behrend&rsquo;s construction of\
  \ large sets of integers without 3-term arithmetic progressions, as well as another\
  \ application of the triangle removal lemma to subsets of a 2-dimensional lattice\
  \ without corners.</p><p>The second half of the lecture discusses further applications\
  \ of the regularity method within graph theory: graph embedding, counting, and removal\
  \ lemmas, as well as a proof of the Erd\u0151s&ndash;Stone&ndash;Simonovits theorem\
  \ on H-free graphs.</p> <p><strong>Instructor:</strong> Yufei Zhao</p>"
course_id: 18-217-graph-theory-and-additive-combinatorics-fall-2019

  <span m="1711970">squared.</span> <span m="1715256">So</span> <span m="1715750">that</span>

  <span m="1716970">theorem.</span> <span m="1719300">Any</span> <span m="1719560">questions?</span></p><p><span

  <span m="2111890">remind</span> <span m="2112280">you,</span> <span m="2112700">was</span>

  <span m="2387310">the</span> <span m="2387410">graph</span> <span m="2387630">embedding</span>
  <span m="2388090">lemma</span> <span m="2388640">says,</span> <span m="2389510">for</span>
  <span m="2389690">example,</span> <span m="2390240">that</span> <span m="2390260">if</span>
  <span m="2390470">H</span> <span m="2390890">is</span> <span m="2391310">bipartite,</span>
  <span m="2395450">and</span> <span m="2396500">with</span> <span m="2396710">maximum</span>

  <span m="2399260">H</span> <span m="2399890">maximum</span> <span m="2400280">degrees</span>

  <span m="2403120">and</span> <span m="2403360">suppose</span> <span m="2405400">you</span>
  <span m="2405520">have</span> <span m="2406090">vertex</span> <span m="2406600">sets</span>
  <span m="2407200">V1</span> <span m="2407740">through</span> <span m="2407980">Vr,</span>
  <span m="2411600">such</span> <span m="2411930">that</span> <span m="2414540">each</span>
  <span m="2414780">vertex</span> <span m="2415170">set</span> <span m="2415500">is</span>
  <span m="2415830">not</span> <span m="2416160">too</span> <span m="2416400">small;</span>
  <span m="2421970">and</span> <span m="2423410">if</span> <span m="2426260">these</span>
  <span m="2426530">vertex</span> <span m="2426930">sets</span> <span m="2427460">are</span>
  <span m="2427720">pairwise</span> <span m="2429200">epsilon</span> <span m="2429620">regular</span>

  <span m="2435170">is</span> <span m="2435710">not</span> <span m="2435920">too</span>
  <span m="2436160">small.</span> <span m="2440890">So</span> <span m="2441480">here</span>
  <span m="2441660">I'm</span> <span m="2442980">assuming</span> <span m="2443430">some</span>
  <span m="2443850">lower</span> <span m="2444100">bound</span> <span m="2444440">on

  <span m="2447240">epsilon.</span> <span m="2450220">Then</span> <span m="2450330">the</span>
  <span m="2450420">conclusion</span> <span m="2452790">is</span> <span m="2452970">that</span>
  <span m="2453240">G</span> <span m="2453720">contains</span> <span m="2456540">a</span>

  <span m="2467110">we</span> <span m="2467200">will</span> <span m="2467320">not</span>
  <span m="2467530">discuss</span> <span m="2467950">the</span> <span m="2468040">proof.</span>
  <span m="2470000">So</span> <span m="2470050">what</span> <span m="2470320">is</span>
  <span m="2470500">this</span> <span m="2471850">hypothesis</span> <span m="2472570">on</span>
  <span m="2473760">H</span> <span m="2473980">being</span> <span m="2474250">r-partite</span>

  <span m="2824100">of</span> <span m="2824280">these</span> <span m="2825270">vertex</span>
  <span m="2825660">set</span> <span m="2825840">sizes</span> <span m="2829530">of</span>
  <span m="2832940">this</span> <span m="2834800">number,</span> <span m="2835290">which</span>
  <span m="2835430">is</span> <span m="2835580">what</span> <span m="2835730">you</span>
  <span m="2835850">would</span> <span m="2836030">predict</span> <span m="2836810">the</span>
  <span m="2836930">number</span> <span m="2837200">of</span> <span m="2837320">embeddings</span>
  <span m="2837800">to</span> <span m="2837920">be</span> <span m="2838880">if</span>
  <span m="2839990">all</span> <span m="2840170">of</span> <span m="2840260">your</span>
  <span m="2840410">bipartite</span> <span m="2840920">graphs</span> <span m="2841400">were</span>
  <span m="2841910">actually</span> <span m="2842600">random.</span></p><p><span m="2856350">So</span>
  <span m="2856550">like</span> <span m="2856760">in</span> <span m="2856850">the</span>
  <span m="2856910">triangle</span> <span m="2857300">counting</span> <span m="2857660">lemma,</span>

  <span m="3703290">basically,</span> <span m="3703710">what</span> <span m="3704160">we've</span>

  <span m="3705570">showed</span> <span m="3705950">that</span> <span m="3706110">if</span>

  <span m="3709980">desired</span> <span m="3710370">quantity</span> <span m="3711300">by,</span>
  <span m="3711600">at</span> <span m="3711750">most,</span> <span m="3712200">an</span>

  <span m="3716130">edge</span> <span m="3716490">of</span> <span m="3716760">H.</span>
  <span m="3718890">Alternatively,</span> <span m="3720030">you</span> <span m="3720150">can</span>

  <span m="4054770">the</span> <span m="4054860">parameters</span> <span m="4055370">somewhat,</span>
  <span m="4056060">so</span> <span m="4056210">remove</span> <span m="4056600">edges,</span>
  <span m="4059640">remove</span> <span m="4060620">low</span> <span m="4060860">density</span>
  <span m="4061310">pairs,</span> <span m="4064610">irregular</span> <span m="4065540">pairs,</span>
  <span m="4068910">and</span> <span m="4069060">small</span> <span m="4069420">vertex</span>
  <span m="4069840">sets.</span></p><p><span m="4074810">And</span> <span m="4075090">the</span>

  <span m="4080310">So</span> <span m="4080430">you</span> <span m="4080640">can</span>
  <span m="4080820">count.</span> <span m="4083020">So</span> <span m="4083310">if</span>
  <span m="4083700">there</span> <span m="4083880">were</span> <span m="4084240">any</span>

  <span m="4176050">So</span> <span m="4176170">what's</span> <span m="4176380">the</span>

  <span m="4447380">has</span> <span m="4448790">strictly</span> <span m="4449240">more</span>
  <span m="4449540">than</span> <span m="4450110">1</span> <span m="4450380">minus</span>

  <span m="4453330">Yeah,</span> <span m="4453770">1</span> <span m="4454210">minus</span>
  <span m="4454510">1</span> <span m="4454810">over r</span> <span m="4455020">times</span>

  <span m="4456670">2</span> <span m="4458540">edges.</span> <span m="4464010">So</span>

  <span m="4469760">theorem</span> <span m="4470570">that</span> <span m="4470780">if</span>
  <span m="4470900">your</span> <span m="4471020">graph</span> <span m="4471350">has</span>

  <span m="4472370">this</span> <span m="4472550">number</span> <span m="4472880">of</span>

  <span m="4484280">in</span> <span m="4484370">particular,</span> <span m="4485000">Turan's</span>
  <span m="4485770">theorem</span> <span m="4486500">implies</span> <span m="4487070">that</span>
  <span m="4488060">G</span> <span m="4488270">prime</span> <span m="4488990">contains</span>
  <span m="4491560">a</span> <span m="4491660">clique</span> <span m="4492290">on</span>
  <span m="4493370">r</span> <span m="4493490">plus</span> <span m="4493760">1</span>
  <span m="4494150">vertices.</span> <span m="4496270">So</span> <span m="4496560">here</span>
  <span m="4497580">I</span> <span m="4497610">should</span> <span m="4497820">say</span>
  <span m="4498360">that</span> <span m="4498570">r</span> <span m="4499530">is</span>
  <span m="4501560">chromatic</span> <span m="4501980">number</span> <span m="4502220">of</span>
  <span m="4502340">H</span> <span m="4503210">minus</span> <span m="4503570">1.</span></p><p><span
  m="4508010">So I</span> <span m="4508100">find</span> <span m="4508430">one</span>
  <span m="4508670">copy</span> <span m="4509300">of</span> <span m="4509420">this</span>
  <span m="4509610">clique,</span> <span m="4512090">but</span> <span m="4512210">what</span>
  <span m="4512360">does</span> <span m="4512510">that</span> <span m="4512630">copy</span>
  <span m="4512990">look</span> <span m="4513170">like?</span> <span m="4517080">I</span>
  <span m="4517170">find</span> <span m="4517620">this</span> <span m="4517830">one</span>
  <span m="4518070">copy</span> <span m="4518550">of</span> <span m="4518700">a</span>
  <span m="4518760">clique.</span> <span m="4523310">Let's</span> <span m="4523460">say</span>
  <span m="4523640">r</span> <span m="4523820">equals</span> <span m="4524120">to</span>
  <span m="4524210">4.</span> <span m="4526650">And</span> <span m="4526740">the</span>
  <span m="4526800">point,</span> <span m="4527820">now,</span> <span m="4528120">is</span>
  <span m="4528310">that</span> <span m="4528540">the</span> <span m="4528990">counting</span>
  <span m="4529440">lemma</span> <span m="4529980">will</span> <span m="4530160">allow</span>
  <span m="4530400">me</span> <span m="4530550">to</span> <span m="4530760">amplify</span>
  <span m="4531990">that</span> <span m="4532260">clique</span> <span m="4533770">into</span>
  <span m="4535000">H.</span> <span m="4544450">So it will</span> <span m="4544790">allow</span>
  <span m="4545000">me</span> <span m="4545120">to</span> <span m="4545210">amplify</span>
  <span m="4546050">this</span> <span m="4546290">clique</span> <span m="4548750">into</span>
  <span m="4549140">a</span> <span m="4549200">copy</span> <span m="4549590">of</span>
  <span m="4549710">H.</span> <span m="4550190">So,</span> <span m="4550370">for</span>

  <span m="4563950">find</span> <span m="4564280">a</span> <span m="4564310">copy</span>
  <span m="4564670">of</span> <span m="4564790">H</span> <span m="4565060">in</span>
  <span m="4565180">G,</span> <span m="4565510">which</span> <span m="4565720">is</span>
  <span m="4565840">what</span> <span m="4565990">we</span> <span m="4566110">want.</span></p><p><span

  <span m="4568160">the</span> <span m="4568250">counting</span> <span m="4568600">lemma</span>

  <span m="4569300">do</span> <span m="4569420">this</span> <span m="4569600">amplification?</span>

  <span m="4587090">turns</span> <span m="4587360">out</span> <span m="4587510">not</span>
  <span m="4587750">to</span> <span m="4587810">be</span> <span m="4587960">an</span>
  <span m="4588080">issue.</span> <span m="4588780">So</span> <span m="4588920">by</span>
  <span m="4589220">counting</span> <span m="4589600">lemma,</span> <span m="4595140">the</span>

  <span m="4602970">considering</span> <span m="4603480">homomorphisms</span> <span

  <span m="4608610">part.</span></p><p><span m="4611380">It's</span> <span m="4611860">at</span>

  <span m="4625900">least</span> <span m="4626830">epsilon</span> <span m="4627310">over</span>
  <span m="4627750">8.</span> <span m="4628480">So</span> <span m="4628690">it's</span>
  <span m="4628810">at</span> <span m="4628900">least</span> <span m="4629620">that</span>

  <span m="4695660">of</span> <span m="4695720">vertices</span> <span m="4696200">of</span>
  <span m="4696360">H.</span> <span m="4699140">But</span> <span m="4699290">I'm</span>
  <span m="4699410">only</span> <span m="4699590">counting</span> <span m="4699920">homomorphisms,</span>

  <span m="4724580">that's</span> <span m="4724760">OK</span> <span m="4725270">because</span>

  <span m="4731870">G</span> <span m="4732380">that</span> <span m="4732560">are</span>
  <span m="4732650">non-injective</span> <span m="4735290">is</span> <span m="4737390">of</span>
  <span m="4737510">a</span> <span m="4737570">lower</span> <span m="4737930">order.</span>
  <span m="4740420">The</span> <span m="4740570">number</span> <span m="4740810">of</span>
  <span m="4740870">non-injective</span> <span m="4741640">maps</span> <span m="4742100">from</span>

  <span m="4743000">well,</span> <span m="4743150">you</span> <span m="4743240">have</span>
  <span m="4743390">to</span> <span m="4743480">pick</span> <span m="4743660">two</span>
  <span m="4743870">vertices</span> <span m="4744260">of</span> <span m="4744350">H</span>
  <span m="4744500">to</span> <span m="4744590">map</span> <span m="4744810">to</span>
  <span m="4744890">the</span> <span m="4744980">same</span> <span m="4745190">vertex,</span>
  <span m="4745880">and</span> <span m="4746000">then</span> <span m="4746140">the</span>
  <span m="4746180">number</span> <span m="4746450">of</span> <span m="4746510">choices,</span>
  <span m="4747050">you</span> <span m="4747170">have</span> <span m="4747800">one</span>
  <span m="4748520">order</span> <span m="4748910">less.</span> <span m="4750750">So</span>
  <span m="4750990">there</span> <span m="4751220">are</span> <span m="4751320">negligible</span>
  <span m="4751950">fraction</span> <span m="4752670">of</span> <span m="4752850">these</span>
  <span m="4753060">homomorphisms.</span></p><p><span m="4756990">And</span> <span
  m="4757090">the</span> <span m="4757150">conclusion,</span> <span m="4757910">then,</span>
  <span m="4758050">is</span> <span m="4758200">that</span> <span m="4758360">G</span>
  <span m="4758500">prime</span> <span m="4759310">contains</span> <span m="4760330">a</span>
  <span m="4760390">copy</span> <span m="4761020">of</span> <span m="4761600">H,</span>
  <span m="4766040">which</span> <span m="4766250">is</span> <span m="4766370">what</span>
  <span m="4766490">we're</span> <span m="4766640">looking</span> <span m="4766910">for.</span>
  <span m="4767050">If G</span> <span m="4767330">prime</span> <span m="4767570">contains</span>
  <span m="4767930">copy</span> <span m="4768200">of</span> <span m="4768280">H,</span>
  <span m="4768480">then G</span> <span m="4768800">contains</span> <span m="4769190">a</span>
  <span m="4769220">copy</span> <span m="4769490">of</span> <span m="4769610">H,</span>
  <span m="4769850">and</span> <span m="4769940">that</span> <span m="4770480">proves</span>
  <span m="4770930">the</span> <span m="4771050">Erdos-Stone-Simonovits</span> <span
  m="4772190">theorem.</span> <span m="4775340">You</span> <span m="4775460">get</span>
  <span m="4775580">a</span> <span m="4775640">bit</span> <span m="4775790">more</span>
  <span m="4775960">out</span> <span m="4776120">of</span> <span m="4776210">this</span>
  <span m="4776360">proof.</span> <span m="4777950">So</span> <span m="4778690">you</span>
  <span m="4778780">see</span> <span m="4778990">that</span> <span m="4779860">not</span>
  <span m="4780220">only</span> <span m="4780550">does</span> <span m="4780820">G</span>
  <span m="4781810">contain</span> <span m="4782950">one</span> <span m="4783250">copy</span>
  <span m="4783640">of</span> <span m="4783760">H,</span> <span m="4784780">but</span>
  <span m="4784910">the</span> <span m="4784990">counting</span> <span m="4785440">lemma</span>
  <span m="4785830">actually</span> <span m="4786130">shows</span> <span m="4786460">you</span>
  <span m="4786700">it</span> <span m="4786790">contains</span> <span m="4787690">many</span>
  <span m="4787990">copies</span> <span m="4788410">of</span> <span m="4788500">H.</span></p><p><span
  m="4790120">And</span> <span m="4790270">this</span> <span m="4790450">is</span>
  <span m="4790600">a</span> <span m="4790660">phenomenon</span> <span m="4791260">known</span>
  <span m="4791590">as</span> <span m="4791650">supersaturation,</span> <span m="4793150">which</span>
  <span m="4793360">you</span> <span m="4793480">already</span> <span m="4793810">saw</span>
  <span m="4794020">in</span> <span m="4794110">the</span> <span m="4794170">first</span>
  <span m="4794440">problem</span> <span m="4794730">set,</span> <span m="4795340">that</span>
  <span m="4795760">often</span> <span m="4796210">when</span> <span m="4796480">you</span>
  <span m="4796690">are</span> <span m="4797020">beyond</span> <span m="4797500">a</span>
  <span m="4797560">certain</span> <span m="4797890">threshold,</span> <span m="4799360">an</span>
  <span m="4799480">extremal</span> <span m="4799960">threshold,</span> <span m="4800950">you</span>
  <span m="4801880">don't</span> <span m="4802120">just</span> <span m="4802390">gain</span>
  <span m="4803020">one</span> <span m="4803410">extra</span> <span m="4803740">copy,</span>
  <span m="4804160">but</span> <span m="4804280">you</span> <span m="4804610">often</span>
  <span m="4804880">gain</span> <span m="4805330">many</span> <span m="4805600">copies.</span>
  <span m="4807570">And</span> <span m="4808390">you</span> <span m="4808540">see</span>
  <span m="4808780">this</span> <span m="4809380">in</span> <span m="4809470">this</span>
  <span m="4809650">proof</span> <span m="4809950">here.</span> <span m="4811790">So</span>
  <span m="4812480">to</span> <span m="4812840">summarize,</span> <span m="4813510">we've</span>
  <span m="4814940">seen</span> <span m="4815450">this</span> <span m="4815630">proof</span>
  <span m="4815990">of</span> <span m="4816490">Erdos-Stone-Simonovits,</span> <span
  m="4818300">which</span> <span m="4818810">comes</span> <span m="4819230">from</span>
  <span m="4820460">applying</span> <span m="4820850">regularity</span> <span m="4821630">and</span>
  <span m="4821780">then</span> <span m="4821990">finding</span> <span m="4822470">a</span>
  <span m="4822530">single</span> <span m="4822920">copy</span> <span m="4823370">of</span>
  <span m="4823580">a</span> <span m="4823850">clique</span> <span m="4824390">from</span>
  <span m="4825000">Turan's</span> <span m="4825370">theorem,</span> <span m="4825980">and</span>
  <span m="4826100">then</span> <span m="4826220">using</span> <span m="4826550">counting</span>

  <span m="4831080">an</span> <span m="4831200">actual</span> <span m="4831560">copy</span>
  <span m="4831950">of</span> <span m="4832190">H.</span></p><p><span m="4835030">So</span>
  <span m="4835220">in</span> <span m="4835370">the</span> <span m="4835610">second</span>
  <span m="4835970">homework,</span> <span m="4836370">one</span> <span m="4836630">of</span>
